Question #250 (ID: 706055)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত | Years: 2016 | Boards:  | Tags: BB
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]y^{x}=9, y^{2}=3^{x}[/math]হলে, [math](x, y)[/math] সমান

Options:
ক. [math](2,3),\left(-2, \frac{1}{9}\right)[/math]
খ. [math](2, \pm 3),\left(-2, \pm \frac{1}{\sqrt{3}}\right)[/math]
গ. [math]\left(2, \frac{1}{9}\right),(-2,-3)[/math]
ঘ. [math]\left(-2,-\frac{1}{9}\right),(2,3)[/math]
ঙ. [math]No \ correct \ answer[/math]


Correct Answer: E.[math]No \ correct \ answer[/math]

Solution:
[math](2, \pm 3),\left(-2, \pm \frac{1}{3}\right)[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l} y^{2}=3^{x} \Rightarrow y=3^{\frac{x}{2}} ; y^{x}=9 \Rightarrow\left(3^{\frac{x}{2}}\right)^{x}=9 \\ \Rightarrow 3^{\frac{x^{2}}{2}}=9 \Rightarrow 3^{\frac{x^{2}}{2}}=3^{2} \Rightarrow \frac{x^{2}}{3}=2 \Rightarrow x=\pm 2 \end{array}[/math]
 [math]x=+2[/math]
 হলে, [math]y^{2}=3^{2} ; y=\pm 3 ; x=-2[/math]
 হলে,[math]y^{2}=3^{-2} ; y=\pm \frac{1}{3} \therefore(x, y)=(2, \pm 3),\left(-2, \pm \frac{1}{3}\right)[/math]


Explanation:

Question:
যদি [math]\log _{\sqrt{8}} x=3 \frac{1}{3}[/math] হয়, তবে [math]x[/math] এর মান কত?

ক. 32
খ. 16
গ. 8
ঘ. 64


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
[math]\log _{\sqrt{8}} x=3 \frac{1}{3} \Rightarrow x=(\sqrt{8})^{3^{\frac{1}{3}}}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l} \Rightarrow x=(\sqrt{8})^{\frac{10}{3}} \Rightarrow x=(8)^{\frac{10}{6}} \Rightarrow x=\left(2^{3}\right)^{\frac{10}{6}} \\ \Rightarrow x=2^{5}=32 \end{array}[/math]

[math]\begin{array}{l}\text{(i) } \log _{a} P=\log _{b} P \times \log _{a} b\\\text{(ii) } \log _{a} \sqrt{a} \times \log _{b} \sqrt{b} \times \log _{c} \sqrt{c}=\frac{1}{8}\\\text{(iii) } \log _{a} b=\frac{1}{\log _{b} a}\end{array}[/math]

নিচের কোনটি সঠিক?

Options:
A. i,ii
B. i,iii
C. ii,iii
D. i,ii,iii


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
[math]\log _{a} \sqrt{a} \times \log _{b} \sqrt{b} \times \log _{c} \sqrt{c}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{2} \log _{a} a \times \frac{1}{2} \log _{b} b \times \frac{1}{2} \log _{c} c=\frac{1}{2} \times \frac{1}{2} \times \frac{1}{2}=\frac{1}{8}[/math]

Question:
[math]x^{x \sqrt{x}}=(x \sqrt{x})^{x}[/math] হলে [math]x[/math] এর মান কত?

Options:
A. [math]\frac{\sqrt{3}}{\sqrt{2}}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{3}{2}[/math]
C. [math]\frac{9}{2}[/math]
D. [math]\frac{9}{4}[/math]


Correct Answer: D.[math]\frac{9}{4}[/math]

Solution:
[math]x^{x \sqrt{x}}=(x \sqrt{x})^{x} \Rightarrow x^{x x^{\frac{1}{2}}}=\left(x \cdot x^{\frac{1}{2}}\right)^{2}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l} \Rightarrow x^{x^{\frac{3}{2}}}=\left(x^{\frac{3}{2}}\right)^{x} \Rightarrow x^{\frac{3}{2}}=\frac{3 x}{2} \Rightarrow x^{\frac{1}{2}}=\frac{3}{2} \\ \Rightarrow x=\frac{3^{2}}{2^{2}}=\frac{9}{4} \end{array}[/math]


Explanation:

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]a^{1}=b, b^{m}=c, c^{n}=a[/math]হলে, [math]Imn[/math] এর মান কত?

Options:
A. [math]abc[/math]
B. [math]\frac{1}{a b c}[/math]
C. [math]1[/math]
D. [math]-1[/math]


Correct Answer: C.[math]1[/math]

Solution:
[math]c^{n}=a \Rightarrow\left(b^{m}\right)^{n}=a \Rightarrow\left\{\left(a^{\prime}\right)^{m}\right\}^{n}=a[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow a^{1 m n}=a^{1} \Rightarrow \operatorname{lmn}=1[/math]

Question #266 (ID: 706071)

Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত | Years: 2015 | Boards:  | Tags: JB
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]M=1+\log _{p} q r[/math] হলে [math]p^M=[/math] কত?

Options:
A. [math]p+q r[/math]
B. [math]1+qr[/math]
C. [math]pqr[/math]
D. [math]qr[/math]


Correct Answer: C.[math]pqr[/math]

Solution:
[math]M=1+\log _{p} q r[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l} \Rightarrow M=\log _{p} q+\log _{p} q r \Rightarrow M=\log _{p} p q r \\ \Rightarrow p^{M}=p q r \end{array}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #268 (ID: 706073)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত | Years: 2015 | Boards:  | Tags: CB
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]a^{x}=b, b^{y}=c[/math] এবং [math]c^{z}=\mathbf{a}[/math] হলে, [math]xyz =[/math] কত?

Options:
A. -1
B. 0
C. 1
D. 2


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
[math]c^{z}=a \Rightarrow\left(b^{y}\right)^{z}=a \Rightarrow\left\{\left(a^{x}\right)^{y}\right\}^{z}=a[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \mathbf{a}^{x y z}=\mathbf{a} \quad \therefore x y z=1[/math]


Explanation:

Question:
[math]\log _{5}\left(\frac{1}{25}\right)[/math] এর মান কত?

Options:
A. 5
B. -5
C. 2
D. -2


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
[math]\log _{5}\left(\frac{1}{25}\right)=\log _{5} \frac{1}{5^{2}}=\log _{5} 5^{-2}[/math]
 [math]=-2 \log _{5} 5=-2[/math]

Question #270 (ID: 706075)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত | Years: 2015 | Boards:  | Tags: CB
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]3^{3 x}=\frac{1}{3}[/math] হলে, x- এর মান কত?

Options:
ক. [math]-3[/math]
খ. [math]\frac{-1}{3}[/math]
গ. [math]\frac{1}{3}[/math]
ঘ. [math]3[/math]


Correct Answer: B.[math]\frac{-1}{3}[/math]

Solution:
[math]3^{3 x}=\frac{1}{3} \Rightarrow 3^{3 x}=3^{-1} \Rightarrow 3 x=-1[/math]
 [math]\therefore x=-\frac{1}{3}[/math]

Question #272 (ID: 706077)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত | Years: 2024, 2016, 2015, 2015 | Boards:  | Tags: JB, ChB, CB, RB
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]a^x=b, b^ y= c[/math] এবং [math]c^z = a[/math] হলে, [math]xyz =[/math] কত?

Options:
A. -1
B. 0
C. 1
D. 2


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
a^x = b, b^y = c এবং c^z = a হয়, তাহলে xyz এর মান হবে 1.

Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা:প্রথম সমীকরণ থেকে আমরা পাই b = a^x.এই b-এর মান দ্বিতীয় সমীকরণে বসালে পাই (a^x)^y = c, অর্থাৎ a^(xy) = c.এখন, c-এর এই মানটি তৃতীয় সমীকরণে বসালে পাই (a^(xy))^z = a.সূচকের নিয়ম অনুযায়ী, a^(xyz) = a.যেহেতু উভয় পক্ষের ভিত্তি a একই, তাই xyz এর মান হবে 1.

Sub-Questions:

Question:
[math]\log _{a} \log _{a} \log _{a}\left(a^{a^{2}}\right)[/math] এর মান কত?

Options:
A. 0
B. 1
C. a
D. -1


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
[math]\log _{a} \log _{a} \log _{a}\left(a^{a}\right)[/math]
 [math]=\log _{a} \log a^{a a} \log a^{a}=\log _{a}^{a} \log _{a}^{a}=1 \times 1=1[/math]


Explanation:

Question #274 (ID: 706079)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত | Years: 2015 | Boards:  | Tags: DiB
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
নিচের তথ্যগুলো লক্ষ কর:

(i) [math]a 
eq 0[/math] হলে [math]a^{0}=1[/math]হবে

(ii) [math]\log _{\sqrt{a}} a \times \log _{\sqrt{b}} b \times \log _{\sqrt{c} c}^{c}=8[/math]হবে

(iii) [math]2^{2 x+1}=243[/math] হলে [math]x = 2[/math] হবে

নিচের কোনটি সঠিক?

Options:
ক. i,ii
খ. i,iii
গ. ii,iii
ঘ. i,ii,iii


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
[math]\log _{\sqrt{a}}(\sqrt{a})^{2} \times \log _{\sqrt{b}}(\sqrt{b})^{2}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l} \times \log _{\sqrt{c}}(\sqrt{c})^{2}=2 \log _{\sqrt{a}} \sqrt{a} \times 2 \log _{\sqrt{b}} \sqrt{b} \\ \times 2 \log _{\sqrt{c}} \sqrt{c}=2 \times 2 \times 2=8 \end{array}[/math]
 [math]x=2[/math]
 বসিয়ে [math]2^{2 \times 2+1}=32[/math]


Explanation:

[math]\log _{a} x=\log _{a} y[/math] হলে নিচের কোনটি সত্য?

Question #307 (ID: 706120)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত | Years: 2019 | Boards:  | Tags: DiB
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]f(x)=\ln \frac{9+x}{9-x}[/math]এর ডোমেন কত?

Options:
A. [math](-\infty, 9)[/math]
B. [math](-9,9)[/math]
C. [math](-9, \infty)[/math]
D. [math](9, \infty)[/math]


Correct Answer: B.[math](-9,9)[/math]

Solution:

[Image]
[math]\frac{9+x}{9-x}>0 ; x>9[/math]
 হলে [math]9+x>0 \& 9-x<0[/math]
 [math]\therefore \frac{9+x}{9-x} 
gtr 0[/math]
 অনুরূপভাবে, [math]x<9[/math]
 হলে, [math]\frac{9+x}{9-x} 
gtr[/math]
 [math]9+x 
eq 0 \Rightarrow x 
eq-9[/math]
 এবং [math]9-x 
eq 0[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \mathrm{x} 
eq 9 \therefore-9<\mathrm{x}<9[/math]


Explanation:

Question #308 (ID: 706121)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত | Years: 2019 | Boards:  | Tags: DiB
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]7^{3 x-6}=5^{3 x-6}[/math]হলে, [math]x[/math] এর মান কত?

Options:
ক. [math]-2[/math]
খ. [math]\frac{1}{2}[/math]
গ. [math]\frac{7}{5}[/math]
ঘ. [math]2[/math]


Correct Answer: D.[math]2[/math]

Solution:
[math]\frac{7^{3 x}}{7^{6}}=\frac{5^{3 x}}{5^{6}} \Rightarrow\left(\frac{7}{5}\right)^{3 x}=\left(\frac{7}{5}\right)^{6}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 3 x=6 \Rightarrow x=2[/math]


Explanation:

Question:
[math]\log _{5} 25+\log _{25} 5=[/math] = কত

Options:
A. [math]1[/math]
B. [math]2[/math]
C. [math]5[/math]
D. [math]\frac{5}{2}[/math]


Correct Answer: D.[math]\frac{5}{2}[/math]

Solution:
[math]\log _{5} 25+\log _{25} 5=\log _{5} 5^{2}+\log _{25} \sqrt{25}[/math]
 [math]=2 \log _{5} 5+\frac{1}{2} \log _{25} 25=2+\frac{1}{2}=\frac{5}{2}[/math]

Question #314 (ID: 705961)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত | Years: 2022 | Boards:  | Tags: CB
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]Logarithm[/math] এর জন্য-
i. [math]\log _{2} 7=\frac{\log _{10} 7}{\log _{10^{2}}}[/math]
ii. [math]\log _{4} 64=4[/math]
iii. [math]\log _{2}\left(\frac{128}{32}\right)=2[/math]
নিচের কোনটি সঠিক?

Options:
A. i ও ii
B. i ও iii
C. ii ও iii
D. i, ii ও iii


Correct Answer: B.i ও iii

Solution:
[math]\text { (i) } \frac{\log _{10^{7}}}{\log _{10^{2}} 2}=\log _{10^{7}} \times \log _{2} 10 x=\log _{2} 7[/math]
 [math]\text { (ii) } \log _{4} 64=\log _{4} 4^{3} \times 3 \log _{4} 4=3 \therefore[/math]
 (ii) সঠিক নয়।[math]\text { (iii) } \log _{2}\left(\frac{128}{32}\right)=\log _{2} 4=\log _{2} 2^{2}=2 \log _{2} 2=2[/math]


Explanation:

Question #317 (ID: 705964)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত | Years: 2021 | Boards:  | Tags: DB
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]A=1-\log _{p}(p q)[/math] হলে, [math]\frac{1}{A}[/math] এর মান কত?

Options:
A. [math]-\log _{q} p[/math]
B. [math]\log _{q} p[/math]
C. [math]\log _{p} q[/math]
D. [math]-\log _{p} q[/math]


Correct Answer: A.[math]-\log _{q} p[/math]

Solution:
[math]A=1-\log _{p}(p q)=\frac{1}{1-\log _{p}(p q)}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l} =\frac{1}{\log _{p} p-\log _{p}(p q)}=\frac{1}{\log _{p}\left(\frac{p}{p q}\right)}=\frac{1}{\log _{p} \frac{1}{q}} \\ =\frac{1}{-\log _{p} q}=-\log _{q} p \end{array}[/math]


Explanation:

D. [math]\frac{2}{3}[/math]

Solution:
[math](p)^{p \sqrt{p}}=\left(p^{\frac{3}{2}}\right)^{p} \Rightarrow p \sqrt{p}=\frac{3}{2} p[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \sqrt{\mathrm{p}}=\frac{3}{2}[/math]

Question #322 (ID: 705969)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত | Years: 2021 | Boards:  | Tags: ChB
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\sqrt[6]{\left(x^{8}\right) \sqrt{\left(x^{6}\right) \sqrt{x^{4}}}}[/math] এর মান নিচের কোনটি?

Options:
A. [math]x[/math]
B. [math]x^2[/math]
C. [math]x^3[/math]
D. [math]x^4[/math]


Correct Answer: B.[math]x^2[/math]

Solution:
[math]\sqrt[6]{x^{8} \sqrt{x^{6} \cdot x^{2}}}=\sqrt[6]{x^{8} \cdot x^{4}}=x^{12 \times \frac{1}{6}}=x^{2}[/math]

Explanation:

Question #323 (ID: 705970)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত | Years: 2021 | Boards:  | Tags: ChB
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
নিচের উদ্দীপকের আলোকে পরবর্তী প্রশ্নের উত্তর দাও:

[math]x^{\frac{1}{p}}=y^{\frac{1}{q}}=z^{\frac{1}{r}}[/math] এবং [math]xyz=1[/math]

নিচের কোনটি সঠিক?

Options:
ক. [math]x=y^{\frac{p}{q}}[/math]
খ. [math]x=y^{\frac{q}{p}}[/math]
গ. [math]y=x^{\frac{r}{q}}[/math]
ঘ. [math]z=y^{\frac{q}{r}}[/math]


Correct Answer: A.[math]x=y^{\frac{p}{q}}[/math]

Solution:
[math]x^{\frac{1}{p}}=y^{\frac{1}{q}} \Rightarrow\left(x^{\frac{1}{p}}\right)^{p}=\left(y^{\frac{1}{q}}\right)^{p} \Rightarrow x=y\frac{p}{q}[/math]

Explanation:

Question #324 (ID: 705971)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত | Years: 2021 | Boards:  | Tags: ChB
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]p+q+r[/math] এর মান নিচের কোনটি?

Options:
ক. [math]0[/math]
খ. [math]1[/math]
গ. [math]xyz[/math]
ঘ. [math]\frac{1}{x}+\frac{1}{y}+\frac{1}{z}[/math]


Correct Answer: A.[math]0[/math]

Solution:
[math]x y z=1 \Rightarrow y^{\frac{P}{q}+1+\frac{r}{q}}=y^{0}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{p+q+r}{q}=0 \Rightarrow p+q+r=0[/math]


Explanation:

খ. [math]8[/math]
গ. [math]27\sqrt{3}[/math]
ঘ. [math]81 \sqrt{3}[/math]


Correct Answer: B.[math]8[/math]

Solution:
[math]\log _{\sqrt{3}} 81=x \Rightarrow(\sqrt{3})^{x}=81 \therefore x=8[/math]

Question:
[math]8^{a}=64^{b}[/math] হলে, [math]a : b[/math] এর মান নিচের কোনটি?

Options:
ক. [math]1:2[/math]
খ. [math]2:1[/math]
গ. [math]2:3[/math]
ঘ. [math]3:2[/math]


Correct Answer: B.[math]2:1[/math]

Solution:
[math]8^{a}=8^{2 b} \Rightarrow a=2 b \Rightarrow \frac{a}{b}=\frac{2}{1}[/math]

Question #327 (ID: 705974)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত | Years: 2021 | Boards:  | Tags: ChB
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]a 
eq 0[/math] এবং [math]\mathrm{m} \in \mathrm{z}, \mathrm{n} \in \mathbb{N}, \mathrm{n}>1[/math] হলে [math](\sqrt[n]{a})^{m}=[/math] কত?

Options:
A. [math]\sqrt[n m]{a}[/math]
B. [math]\sqrt[m]{a}[/math]
C. [math]\sqrt[n]{a^{m}}[/math]
D. [math]\frac{1}{a^{m n}}[/math]


Correct Answer: C.[math]\sqrt[n]{a^{m}}[/math]

Solution:
[math](\sqrt[n]{a})^{m}=\left(a^{\frac{1}{n}}\right)^{m}=a^{\frac{m}{n}}[/math]
 [math]=\left(a^{m}\right)^{\frac{1}{n}}=\sqrt[n]{a^{m}}[/math]


Explanation:

Solution:

D. [math]64 a^{3}[/math]

Solution:

Question #331 (ID: 705978)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত | Years: 2021 | Boards:  | Tags: BB
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]f(x)=2^{x}[/math] হলে–

(i) এটি [math](0, 1)[/math] বিন্দুগামী

(ii) এর ডোমেন [math](-\infty, \infty)[/math]

(iii) এর রেঞ্জ [math](0, \infty)[/math]

নিচের কোনটি সঠিক?

Options:
A. i,ii
B. i,iii
C. ii,iii
D. i,ii,iii


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
[math](i)x=0[/math]
 হলে [math]y=1 \ \therefore (0,1)[/math]
 বন্দুগামী, যা সত্য [math](ii)y=2^x[/math]
 এর [math]Dom=((-\infty, \infty))[/math]
 এবং [math](iii)[/math]
 রেঞ্জ [math](0,\infty)[/math]


Explanation:

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\log _{x} 4+\log _{x} 8=5[/math] হলে, [math]x[/math] এর মান কত?

Options:
ক. 2
খ. 4
গ. 8
ঘ. 32


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
[math]\log _{x} 4+\log _{x} 8=\log _{x}(4 \times 8)=\log _{x} 32=5 \Rightarrow x^{5}=32=2^{5} \therefore x=2[/math]

খ. [math]\frac{2}{3}[/math]

ঘ. [math]\frac{5}{2}[/math]

Question #334 (ID: 705981)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত | Years: 2021 | Boards:  | Tags: BB
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
নিচের উদ্দীপকের আলোকে পরবর্তী প্রশ্নের উত্তর দাও :

[math]y=3^x[/math]

যদি [math]\log _{\sqrt{3}} y=z[/math]হয়, তবে [math]\frac{z}{x}[/math]এর মান কত?

Options:
ক. [math]\frac{1}{3}[/math]
খ. [math]\frac{1}{2}[/math]
গ. [math]2[/math]
ঘ. [math]3[/math]


Correct Answer: C.[math]2[/math]

Solution:
[math]\log _{\sqrt{3}} y=z \Rightarrow \log _{\sqrt{3}} 3^{x}=z[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l} \Rightarrow 3^{x}=\sqrt{3}^{z} \Rightarrow(\sqrt{3})^{2 x}=(\sqrt{3})^{z} \\ \Rightarrow 2 x=z \Rightarrow \frac{z}{x}=2 \end{array}[/math]


Explanation:

Question:
[math]\sqrt[13]{\left(x^{6}\right) \sqrt[2]{\left(x^{16}\right) \sqrt[3]{x^{18}}}}=[/math] কত?

Options:
A. [math]X \frac{17}{13}[/math]
B. [math]x^{\frac{13}{17}}[/math]
C. [math]x^{\frac{19}{13}}[/math]
D. [math]x^{\frac{13}{19}}[/math]


Correct Answer: A.[math]X \frac{17}{13}[/math]

Solution:
[math]\sqrt[13]{\left(x^{6}\right) \sqrt[2]{\left(x^{16}\right) \sqrt[3]{x^{18}}}}=\sqrt[13]{x^{6} \sqrt[2]{x^{16} \cdot x^{6}}}=\sqrt[13]{x^{17}}=x^{\frac{17}{13}}[/math]

B. [math]1:2[/math]
C. [math]2:1[/math]
D. [math]3:1[/math]


Correct Answer: A.[math]1:3[/math]

Solution:
[math]4^{\frac{1}{x}}=\left(4^{3}\right)^{\frac{1}{y}} \Rightarrow \frac{1}{x}=\frac{3}{y} \Rightarrow \frac{x}{y}=\frac{1}{3}[/math]

Question #339 (ID: 705986)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত | Years: 2020 | Boards:  | Tags: JB
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]y=1-5^{-x}[/math]এর বিপরীত ফাংশন নিচের কোনটি?

Options:
ক. [math]\log _{5}(1-x)[/math]
খ. [math]1-5^x[/math]
গ. [math]\log _{5}\left(\frac{1}{1-x}\right)[/math]
ঘ. [math]\log _{5}(x-1)[/math]


Correct Answer: C.[math]\log _{5}\left(\frac{1}{1-x}\right)[/math]

Solution:
[math]y=1-5^{-x} ; 5^{-x}=1-y[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l} \Rightarrow \log _{5}(1-y)=-x \Rightarrow x=-\log _{5}(1-y) \\ \Rightarrow x=\log _{5} \frac{1}{1-y} \therefore f^{-1}(x)=\log _{5} \frac{1}{1-x} \end{array}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #341 (ID: 705988)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত | Years: 2020 | Boards:  | Tags: JB
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]f(x)=\frac{x}{|x|}[/math]ফাংশনটির রেঞ্জ নিচের কোনটি? (যখন [math]x 
eq 0[/math] )

Options:
ক. [math]R_{f}=\{1\}[/math]
খ. [math]R_{f}=\{-1\}[/math]
গ. [math]R_{f}=\{x: x \in R\}[/math]
ঘ. [math]\mathrm{R}_{\mathrm{f}}=\{-1,1\}[/math]


Correct Answer: D.[math]\mathrm{R}_{\mathrm{f}}=\{-1,1\}[/math]

Solution:
[math]|x|=\left\{\begin{array}{r} -x, x<0 \\ x, x \geq 0 \end{array} \quad \therefore f(x)=\frac{x}{x}\right.=1[/math]
 অথবা [math]\mathrm{f}(\mathrm{x})=\frac{\mathrm{x}}{-\mathrm{x}}=-1 \quad \therefore \mathrm{R}_{\mathrm{f}}=\{1,-1\}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #342 (ID: 705989)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত | Years: 2021 | Boards:  | Tags: CB
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]p = q = 0,[/math] হলে [math]ab + bc = ?[/math]

Options:
A. [math]0[/math]
B. [math]1[/math]
C. [math]2[/math]
D. [math]3[/math]


Correct Answer: C.[math]2[/math]

Solution:
[math]P=\log _{a} b c=0 \Rightarrow b c=a^{e}=1\text { Similarly.q }=0[/math]
 হও্যায় [math]ab=1[/math]
 [math]\therefore a b+b c=1+1=2[/math]


Explanation:

Question #343 (ID: 705990)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত | Years: 2020 | Boards:  | Tags: CB
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\log _{\sqrt{27}} y=1 \frac{1}{3}[/math] হলে [math]y[/math] এর মান কত?

Options:
A. [math]3^{\frac{1}{3}}[/math]
B. [math]3^{\frac{3}{2}}[/math]
C. [math]9[/math]
D. [math]36[/math]


Correct Answer: C.[math]9[/math]

Solution:
[math]\log _{\sqrt{27}} y=1 \frac{1}{3}=\frac{4}{3} \Rightarrow y=(\sqrt{27})^{\frac{4}{3}}=3^{\frac{3}{2} \times \frac{4}{3}}=3^{2}=9[/math]

Explanation:

C. [math]a^{\frac{1}{2}}[/math]
D. [math]a^0[/math]


Correct Answer: C.[math]a^{\frac{1}{2}}[/math]

Solution:

ক. 16
খ. 4
গ. 2
ঘ. 1


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
[math]\log _{2} \log _{2} \log _{2} 16[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l} =\log _{2} \log _{2}\left(4 \log _{2} 2\right)=\log _{2} \log _{2} 4 \\ =\log _{2}\left(2 \log _{2} 2\right)=\log _{2} 2=1 \end{array}[/math]

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\sqrt[24]{\left(x^{9}\right) \sqrt{x^{6}}}[/math]এর মান নিচের কোনটি?

Options:
A. [math]\sqrt{x}[/math]
B. [math]x[/math]
C. [math]x \sqrt{x}[/math]
D. [math]x^2[/math]


Correct Answer: A.[math]\sqrt{x}[/math]

Solution:
[math]\sqrt[24]{\left(x^{9}\right) \sqrt{x^{6}}}=\sqrt[24]{x^{9} \times x^{3}}=x^{\frac{12}{24}}=x^{\frac{1}{2}}=\sqrt{x}[/math]

Explanation:

Question #351 (ID: 705998)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত | Years: 2020 | Boards:  | Tags: MB
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]f(x)=\ln \frac{1-x}{1+x}[/math] এর বিপরীত ফাংশন কোনটি?

Options:
ক. [math]\frac{1+e^{y}}{e^{y}}[/math]
খ. [math]\frac{e^{y}}{1-e^{y}}[/math]
গ. [math]\frac{1+e^{y}}{1-e^{y}}[/math]
ঘ. [math]\frac{1-e^{y}}{1+e^{y}}[/math]


Correct Answer: D.[math]\frac{1-e^{y}}{1+e^{y}}[/math]

Solution:
[math]y=\ln \frac{1-x}{1+x} ; e^{y}=\frac{1-x}{1+x}[/math]
 [math]\frac{e^{y}+1}{e^{y}-1}=\frac{2}{-2 x} ; \frac{e^{y}-1}{e^{y}+1}=-x \quad \therefore x=\frac{1-e^{y}}{1+e^{y}}[/math]


Explanation:


Sub-Questions:

================================================================================
Question #352 (ID: 705999)

Question:
[math]4^{x}=8^{y}[/math]হলে, [math]\frac{x}{y}[/math] এর মান কত?

Options:
ক. [math]2[/math]
খ. [math]\frac{3}{2}[/math]
গ. [math]\frac{2}{3}[/math]
ঘ. [math]\frac{1}{2}[/math]


Correct Answer: B.[math]\frac{3}{2}[/math]

Solution:
[math]4^{x}=8^{y}[/math]
 [math]2^{2 x}=2^{3 y}, 2 x=3 y\Rightarrow \frac{x}{y}=\frac{3}{2}[/math]

Question #353 (ID: 706000)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত | Years: 2019 | Boards:  | Tags: DB
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]F(x)=\frac{|x|}{x-3}[/math] ফাংশনটির ডোমেন কত?

Options:
ক. [math]\{\mathrm{x}: \mathrm{x} \in \mathbb{R}[/math] এবং [math]x>3\}[/math]
খ. [math]\{x: x \in \mathbb{R}[/math] এবং [math]x<3\}[/math]
গ. [math]\{x: x \in \mathbb{R}[/math] এবং [math]x=3\}[/math]
ঘ. [math]\{x: x \in \mathbb{R}[/math] এবং [math]x \neq 3\}[/math]


Correct Answer: D.[math]\{x: x \in \mathbb{R}[/math] এবং [math]x \neq 3\}[/math]

Solution:
প্রদত্ত ফাংশন [math]f(x)=\frac{|x|}{x-3}[/math]
 তে [math]x = 3[/math]
 হলে ফাংশনটিকে আর সংজ্ঞায়িত করা যায় না। তাই ডোমনে সকল বাস্তব সংখ্যা হবে কিন্তু [math]x = 3[/math]
 হতে পারবে না।

Explanation:

Question #354 (ID: 706001)

Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত | Years: 2021 | Boards:  | Tags: MB

Question:
[math]25^{3 x}=5^{x+1}[/math] হলে [math]x[/math] এর মান কত?

Options:
ক. [math]\frac{1}{8}[/math]
খ. [math]\frac{1}{5}[/math]
গ. [math]\frac{1}{4}[/math]
ঘ. [math]\frac{1}{2}[/math]


Correct Answer: B.[math]\frac{1}{5}[/math]

Solution:
[math]\left(5^{2}\right)^{3 x}=5^{x+1} \Rightarrow 6 x=x+1[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow x=\frac{1}{5}[/math]

Question #355 (ID: 706002)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত | Years: 2019 | Boards:  | Tags: DB
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]f(x)=\left(\frac{1}{2}\right)^{x}[/math]একটি সূচকীয় ফাংশন হলে-

(i) এটি [math](0,1)[/math] বিন্দুগামী

(ii) এর ডোমেন [math](-\infty, \infty)[/math]

(iii) এর রেঞ্জ [math](0, \infty)[/math]

নিচের কোনটি সঠিক?

Options:
ক. i,ii
খ. i,iii
গ. ii,iii
ঘ. i,ii,iii


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
ধরি, [math]y=f(x)=\left(\frac{1}{2}\right)^{x}[/math]
 একটি সূচকীয় ফাংশন দেও্যা আছে।(i) যখন [math]x = 0[/math]
; তখন [math]\left(\frac{1}{2}\right)^{0}=1[/math]
 সুতরাং [math](0,1)[/math]
 রেখার উপর একটি বিন্দু।(ii) যখন x এর ধনাত্মক বা ঋণাত্মক মানের জন্য f(x) সর্বদা ধনাত্বক। [math]\therefore[/math]
 ডোমেন [math](-\infty, \infty)[/math]
 এবং রেঞ্জ [math](0, \infty)[/math]


Explanation:

Question #356 (ID: 706003)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত | Years: 2021 | Boards:  | Tags: MB
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\log _{3} 15-\log _{3} 5=?[/math]

Options:
A. [math]\log _{3} 10[/math]
B. [math]\log _{3} 75[/math]
C. [math]1[/math]
D. [math]27[/math]


Correct Answer: C.[math]1[/math]

Solution:
[math]\log _{3}(3 \times 5)-\log _{3} 5[/math]
 [math]=\log _{3} 3+\log _{3} 5-\log _{3} 5=\log _{3} 3=1[/math]


Explanation:

Question #357 (ID: 706004)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত | Years: 2019 | Boards:  | Tags: RB
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\log _{\sqrt{8}} 4[/math]এর মান কত?

Options:
A. [math]8[/math]
B. [math]2[/math]
C. [math]\frac{4}{3}[/math]
D. [math]\frac{3}{4}[/math]


Correct Answer: C.[math]\frac{4}{3}[/math]

Solution:
ধরি, [math]\log _{\sqrt{8}} 4=x \Rightarrow(\sqrt{8})^{x}=4[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow\left(2^{\frac{3}{2}}\right)^{x}=2^{2} \Rightarrow \frac{3 x}{2}=2 \Rightarrow x=\frac{4}{3}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #359 (ID: 706006)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত | Years: 2019 | Boards:  | Tags: RB
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\sqrt[3]{a^{5}}=2 \sqrt[6]{a^{7}}[/math] হলে, [math]a[/math] এর মান কত?

Options:
A. [math]1[/math]
B. [math]\sqrt{2}[/math]
C. [math]2[/math]
D. [math]4[/math]


Correct Answer: D.[math]4[/math]

Solution:
[math]a^{\frac{5}{3}}=2 \times a^{\frac{7}{6}} \Rightarrow a^{\frac{5}{3}-\frac{7}{6}}=2[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow a^{\frac{1}{2}}=2 \Rightarrow a=4[/math]


Explanation:

Question:
লগারিদমীয় এবং সূচকীয় ফাংশনের মধ্যে পার্থক্য কি?
